		function checkTitle () {
			var l = $$("subject").value.replace(/[^\x00-\xff]/gi, "xx").length;
			if(60 < l/2){
				$("#titleTips").html('您已经超过<i id="titleLength" style="color:red">' + Math.abs(60 - (l/2)) + '</i>字');
			}else{
				$("#titleTips").html('您还可以输入<i id="titleLength" style="color:black">' + Math.abs( (l/2)-60) + '</i>字');
			}
		}
		function selType(obj,hideObj){
			var hideObj = document.getElementById(hideObj);
			var aObjs = obj.parentNode.getElementsByTagName("a");	
			if(obj.className == "selected"){
				obj.className = "";	
				hideObj.value = "";
			}else{
				for(var j=0,len=aObjs.length;j<len;j++){
					aObjs[j].className = "";
				}
				obj.className = "selected";
				hideObj.value = obj.innerHTML;
			}
			$(obj).blur();

		var ArrayMap = function() {
			this.keys = [];
			this.values = [];
		}

		ArrayMap.prototype = {
			get:function(key) {
				return this.values[key];
			},
			put:function(key,val) {
				if (this.values[key] == null) {
					this.keys.push(key);
				}
				this.values[key] = val;
			},
			remove:function(key) {
				if (this.values[key] == null) {
					return;
				}
				for ( var m in this.keys) {
					if (this.keys[m] == key) {
						this.keys.splice(m,1);
					}
				}
			},
			each:function(fn) {
				if (typeof fn != 'function') {
					return;
				}
				for (var m in this.keys) {
					fn(this.keys[m],this.get(this.keys[m]),m) ;
				}
			},
			sizes:function() {
				return this.keys.length;
			}
		}

		function getUploadCookie(name,nounescape) {
				var cookie_start = document.cookie.indexOf(name);
				var cookie_end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", cookie_start);
				if(cookie_start == -1) {
					return '';
				} else {
					var v = document.cookie.substring(cookie_start + name.length + 1, (cookie_end > cookie_start ? cookie_end : document.cookie.length));
					return !nounescape ? unescape(v) : v;
				}
		}
		
		function getCookie(name) { 
		    var arr,reg=new RegExp("(^| )"+name+"=([^;]*)(;|$)");
		 
		    if(arr=document.cookie.match(reg))
		        return unescape(arr[2]); 
		    else 
		        return null; 
		}

		function otherControlpos() {
						if (enableautoheight) {
									var uploadWrap = document.getElementById("uploadWrap");
									var controlObj = document.getElementById("e_controls");
									var tmpWrapHeight = $(uploadWrap).height();
									var tmpEditorHeight = $("#editor").height();
									var docScrollTop = $(document).scrollTop();
									var tmpEditorOffsetTop = $("#editor").offset().top;
									if (controlObj.className.indexOf("uploadFix")>-1){
										uploadWrap.style.marginTop =  "0px";
											if (docScrollTop + tmpWrapHeight - tmpEditorOffsetTop >  tmpEditorHeight) {
													uploadWrap.style.position = uploadWrap.style.top = '';
													uploadWrap.className = 'uploadCommon imgupload';
													uploadWrap.style.marginTop = (tmpEditorHeight - tmpWrapHeight) + "px";
											} else {
													uploadWrap.className = 'mTop uploadFix imgupload ';
											}
									} else {
											uploadWrap.className = 'mTop uploadCommon imgupload ';
									}
						}

		}

	$("#J-troDes .showall").toggle(function(){
	$("#J-troDes").addClass("pAbs");
	$("#infoTxt").html($textA);
	$("#J-troDes .showall").addClass("hidden").html("收起");
	},function(){
		$("#J-troDes").removeClass("pAbs");
		$("#infoTxt").html($curTxt);
		$("#J-troDes .showall").removeClass("hidden").html("展开");
	}); 
})


function loadComment(params){
	var htmls = '<div style="background-color:#FFFFFF; border:1px solid #000000;height:30px; line-height:30px; width:200px; vertical-align:middle"><table cellpadding="0" border="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" height="100%"><tr><td valign="middle" align="center" width="50"><img src="http://www1.pclady.com.cn/images/shaike/071105/wait.gif" width="20" height="20" /></td><td><b>正在加载...</b></td></tr></table></div>';
	$.ajax({
           url: "/common/2013/solr_comment_list.jsp?&pageType=1&"+params,
           cache: true,
           dataType: "html",
           beforeSend: function(html) {
               $.blockUI({
                   message: htmls,
                   css:{width:'200px',height:'30px'}
               });
           },
           success: function(html) {
               $.unblockUI();
               $("#comment_detail").html(html);
               if (window.location.hash) {
                   window.location.href = window.location.href.substring(0, window.location.href.indexOf('#')) + '#productFilter';
               } else {
                   window.location.href = window.location.href + '#productFilter';
               }
           }
       });
}
function clogin(){

	//指定当前 URL. 
	document.getElementById("return").value = "http://cosme.pclady.com.cn/action/login.jsp?return=http://cosme.pclady.com.cn/product/82067.html#comment_area";
	myPop=new myPopup("#PopBox",".Mask",".PopClose");  
    myPop.pup();
	return;
}

function commentUpButton(at, id){
	var numOld = $("#"+id).html();
	$.ajax({
		url : "/common/ajax/_product_like.jsp?id=82067&at="+at,
		dataType : "json",
		success: function(resp) {
			if(resp.actionNum<3){
				if(resp.num>0){
					$("#"+id).html("("+resp.num+")");
				}
			}else{
				$("#"+id).html(numOld);
				document.getElementById (id).onclick = function(){}
			}
        }
	});
}


	function quickComment(pId) {
    	var content = $("#kuaisu_textarea").val();
    	if(content.length>50){
    		tipsMsg("您填写的内容超过50字，请适当删减后再提交");
    	}else{
		var htmls = '<div style="background-color:#FFFFFF; border:1px solid #000000;height:30px; line-height:30px; width:200px; vertical-align:middle"><table cellpadding="0" border="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" height="100%"><tr><td valign="middle" align="center" width="50"><img src="http://www1.pclady.com.cn/images/shaike/071105/wait.gif" width="20" height="20" /></td><td><b>评论提交中...</b></td></tr></table></div>';
		$.ajax({
			url : "/comment/action/quickComment.jsp",
			cache : true,
			dataType : "json",
			data : {
				content : encodeURI(content),
				id : pId
			},
			beforeSend : function(html) {
				$.blockUI({
					message : htmls,
					css : {
						width : '200px',
						height : '30px'
					}
				});
			},

			success : function(resp) {
				$.unblockUI();
				$("#kuaisu_textarea").val("");
				tipsMsg(resp.msg);
			}
		});
    	}
	}
	function blockOpen(u, w, h) {
		var html = '<iframe src="' + u + '" frameborder="0" width="' + w
				+ '" height="' + h + '" scrolling="no"></iframe>';
		$.blockUI( {
			message : html,
			css : {
				width : w + 'px',
				height : h + 'px'
			}
		})
	}
	function blockClose(b) {
		$.unblockUI();
		if (b)
			window.location.reload(false)
	}
	function feedback(productId) {
	    blockOpen('http://cosme.pclady.com.cn/product/feedback.jsp?pid=' + productId, 570, 552);
	}
	var hasLogIn = false;
	function collectP(){
		if (!hasLogIn){
			myPop=new myPopup("#PopBox",".Mask",".PopClose");  
		    myPop.pup();
			return;
		}
		$.ajax({
			url: 'http://cosme.pclady.com.cn/action/wantByNum_do.jsp',
			type: 'POST',
			async: false,
			data: {
				productId: 82067
				},
			dataType: 'json',
	        success: function(response){
	        	if (response.code == 0){
	        		tipsMsg("收藏成功!您可以到小窝查看更多的收藏，<a href=\"http://my.pclady.com.cn/user/component/comment/myComment.jsp?pageType=1\" target=\"_blank\">查看>>></a>");
	        		$("#want_button").html("<a href=\"javascript:void(0);\" class=\"collectBtn pink\">已收藏</a>");
	        	} else {
	        		tipsMsg(response.message);
	        	}
	        },
	        error: function(xhr){
	        	tipsMsg("失败");
	        }
		});
	}
